! targeting adult ad elements visible on Arabic/Middle-East
! websites. It is a PROTECTIVE filter designed to hide
! remaining adult ad containers, overlays, banners, popups,

! - EasyList / EasyPrivacy
! - uBlock Origin's built-in filter lists
! - AdGuard's filter lists
! - Network-level blocking (DNS, Pi-hole, etc.)
! Report issues: https://github.com/1dm-adblock/issues
! Title: 1DM Mobile & Push Notification Adult Ad Blocker
! Version: 2026.04.13
! Last modified: 13 Apr 2026
! Expires: 3 days
! Licence: https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by-nc-sa/4.0/
! DESCRIPTION: Blocks adult advertising delivered through mobile SDKs,
! push notification services, in-app ad networks, mobile-optimized ad
! delivery, WebView injection, and mobile pop-under/redirect networks.
! PROTECTIVE FILTER — prevents adult content from reaching mobile devices.
! CATEGORIES:
!   1. Mobile Adult Ad SDKs (Android/iOS)
!   2. Push Notification Services (Adult Content)
!   3. In-App Adult Ad Networks
!   4. Mobile Web Pop-Under Networks
!   5. WebView Ad Injection for Adult Content
!   6. Mobile Redirect Ad Networks
!   7. Adult Mobile Ad Exchanges
